18-20 Point Modern Decklists
============================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 7, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











A total of 50 players earned 18 or 19 points in the Modern rounds of Pro Tour *Oath of the Gatewatch*. There were 49 players who earned 18 points (6-4) from Modern and just one who earned 19 points (6-3-1). No one earned 20 points.




---

#### The following player finished with 19 points (6-3-1) in Modern:







#### Carlos Martinez


##### 




![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
